- **Pro bono / favor economy** — approximately 10%. Calls from former colleagues, from neighborhood contacts, from the small number of clergy and social workers she has known long enough to have built mutual-debt with.

### 2.2 The Office

A second-floor walk-up above a Caribbean takeout in a Harlem block she has worked off-and-on for two decades. Single door, no signage, reinforced steel core behind a wood veneer. One window, north-facing, fitted with security film and an interior steel mesh she installed herself in a weekend. Two rooms: front office (desk, two client chairs, low file cabinet, a corkboard she still actually uses for active-case linking despite owning the software), back room (cot, hot plate, small refrigerator, a heavy bag suspended from a structural beam reinforced with bracketry she also installed herself).

Desk-side drawer, top right: backup sidearm, holstered, condition-three. Drawer below: cleaning kit, spare magazines, a sealed envelope of cash in twenties she has not opened in eleven months (analyst inference from the dust line). Drawer below that: a small medical kit substantially better-stocked than what she carries on her person, including tourniquets, hemostatic gauze, and ampoules of a prosthesis-interface lubricant she orders from a third-party vendor because she has not been back to Stark service for over four years.

The corkboard has, at any given time, photographs of between three and six missing persons, pinned by neighborhood. She rotates them out only when closed.

### 2.3 The Residence

A one-bedroom apartment in a co-op building she part-owns through a shell entity, two subway stops from the office. She does not sleep there reliably; current estimate from observed lighting patterns is that she spends three to four nights a week on the office cot and the remainder at the apartment. The apartment is the more *furnished* space — books, a couch, framed photographs (Colleen, a small one of her late mother, a group shot from the early Knightwing era that includes Danny) — but the office is where she lives in the operational sense.

Colleen Wing's apartment is approximately fourteen minutes' walk from the subject's, and she is documented there at least one evening per week, sometimes overnight on the spare couch when Colleen has been training late.

---

## 3. Relational Topography, Present Tense

### 3.1 Colleen Wing

The load-bearing wall. The relationship has, if anything, *deepened* in the current era as Misty's organizational scaffolding has contracted around it. They speak daily — short calls, mostly, operational and logistical, the texture of long-married people running a shared life across two addresses. They train together two to three times a week at Colleen's dojo: light sparring on Mondays, weapons work (Misty practicing edged-weapon defense against Colleen's sword, an exercise that is also a controlled exposure to the kind of close-quarters somatic vulnerability she otherwise avoids) on Wednesdays, heavy bag and conditioning on Fridays.

This is the only relationship in the subject's life where she is consistently observed initiating physical contact for non-operational reasons — a hand on Colleen's shoulder, a hip-check in the kitchen, the small unselfconscious touch that the rest of her interpersonal repertoire has been engineered to avoid. The defensive architecture has one door, and Colleen walks through it.

### 3.2 Danny Rand

Reduced contact, warm valence. They are no longer romantic partners and have not been for some time. The current relationship reads as elder-sibling-coded, with Misty continuing to occupy the stabilizing role she always did but at lower frequency and without the performance burden of intimacy. She takes his calls. She refers cases to him when the matter is mystical or martial in a way she cannot service. She has not been to K'un L'un and would not go. She tracks his whereabouts loosely; this analyst assesses she could locate him within six hours from a cold start.

### 3.3 Luke Cage

Stable peer relationship, professionally weighted. Luke's institutional ascension (mayoral arc, civic roles, parental commitments to Danielle) has structurally moved him out of the same operational space the subject occupies, and she treats this with respect rather than abandonment-coded protest — a notable contrast to how she has historically processed male partners moving away. She is on the short list of people Luke calls when something needs to be handled outside the channels his current role permits. She is also, observably, on the *very* short list permitted to hold Danielle Cage unsupervised, a privilege not extended lightly in that household.

### 3.4 Sam Wilson

Intermittent contact, mutual-respect coded, occasional case overlap. Romantic history acknowledged on both sides as historical. No current intimacy.

### 3.5 The NYPD Diaspora

She maintains, by this analyst's count, eleven active law-enforcement contacts — eight retired, three still serving — across NYPD, Port Authority, and one federal. These are the *connections* infrastructure that makes her investigative practice viable. Each is maintained through a documented pattern of small, regular, reciprocal exchanges: a referral here, a drink there, a courtesy heads-up on a name she has surfaced. She forgets none of these obligations and lets none of them lapse.

She does not, in the current era, drink with active police. She drinks with the retired ones.

### 3.6 The Neighborhood

A category the file should not collapse into "contacts." The subject is *known* on her blocks — by the takeout owner downstairs, by the building super, by a specific bodega owner three doors east who saves her the Sunday paper, by two of the working girls whose corner falls within her sightline and to whom she has provided, at various points, transportation, a place to make a phone call, and the name of a lawyer. None of these relationships are professionally productive in a billable sense. All of them are part of how she lives.

### 3.7 Family of Origin

Mother deceased (pre-arm-loss; this analyst flags the timing as part of the etiology of her response to the amputation — the maternal scaffolding was already gone). A sister, geographically distant, contact intermittent and tonally affectionate but not close. No children. No ex-spouse.

---

## 4. Somatic and Psychiatric Status, Present

### 4.1 The Body

The kinetic mismatch documented in §2 of the prior workup has now been a chronic load for the bulk of her adult life. Present-tense observable findings:

- **Standing posture:** mild forward carriage of the right shoulder, compensatory left-shoulder elevation, head-forward at approximately 1–2 cm beyond neutral. Consistent with the predicted cervical and thoracic strain pattern.
- **Gait:** unremarkable at walking pace; under load (running, stairs at speed), a faint favoring of the right side that this analyst reads as anticipatory protection of the prosthesis-spine interface rather than acute pain.
- **Sleep:** estimated five to six hours nightly, fragmented, with a consistent 3:00–4:00 a.m. waking pattern observable in lighting-cycle data from both residence and office. She does not return to sleep quickly; the 4:00–5:00 a.m. window is the most consistent "she is awake and doing paperwork" hour in her schedule.
- **Diet:** functional, not maintained. The Caribbean takeout downstairs is approximately 30% of her caloric intake. Coffee is the consistent variable; she drinks it through the day and stops late enough to be implicated in the sleep pattern.
- **Alcohol:** moderate, episodic, currently trending *slightly upward* from the prior decade's baseline by this analyst's read — explainable by the increased solitary time the contracted operation has produced. Not yet at dependence threshold. Worth monitoring.
- **Prosthesis:** unserviced through institutional channels for over four years. She has maintained it competently — she knows the limb better than any technician would — but the neural-interface degradation curve for a Stark-era unit at this service interval is non-trivial. Inference: she is aware of this and avoiding it. Reasons (analyst's read): a service appointment would require admitting the limb is not invulnerable, which is a category of admission her defensive architecture is structured to refuse.

### 4.2 The Mind

The subsyndromal PTSD picture documented previously remains stable. Avoidance and numbing cluster: robust. Intrusion cluster: still suppressed in observable behavior; this analyst maintains the assessment that intrusions exist and are managed by the operational tempo. The current contracted tempo is the first sustained test of this hypothesis in her adult life, and the 3:00 a.m. waking pattern is, by this analyst's reading, the first observable leak.

Affect baseline: governed. Humor intact. The "tired" coloring noted in modern-era depictions has not resolved and is, mildly, more pronounced.

She has not sought mental health care. She would not. If asked whether she should, she would deflect with humor and change the subject within two exchanges. This analyst's confidence in that prediction is high.

### 4.3 What Has Improved

To be fair to the subject and to the record: she has, in the current era, made several quiet adjustments that read as proto-therapeutic without being labeled as such. The training cadence with Colleen is more regular and more deliberately *recovery-oriented* than in prior eras (longer warm-ups, more attention to mobility, Colleen has clearly negotiated this in increments). The case mix has shifted toward work that is meaningful to her in ways billable hours alone do not explain. The neighborhood embedding is denser than it has been since the original Knightwing storefront era. She is, in this analyst's view, *self-prescribing connection* at a low dose she will not admit is medicine.

---

## 5. Daily and Weekly Pattern, Current

Reconstructed from observation, declared statements, and pattern inference. Variance high; the skeleton is consistent.

**Weekday, office night:**
04:00 — wakes, does not move for several minutes, then rises. Coffee. Paperwork at the desk, low lamp. Two hours of the most productive cognitive work of her day.
06:30 — calisthenics in the back room, modified for the kinetic mismatch (no overhead pressing with the prosthesis, no full burpees; she does push variations, core work, and shadow boxing with the prosthesis at deliberately reduced output).
07:30 — shower at the office (a small stall installed in the back-room closet). Dresses.
08:15 — coffee and food from downstairs, eaten at the desk while she scans the local police blotter, two specific neighborhood newsletters she pays attention to, and her encrypted message queue.
09:00–12:00 — client work, calls, the connections-keeping labor.
12:00–14:00 — field time, typically. Tails, interviews, document service, courthouse visits.
14:00–17:00 — second tranche of field time or office-based investigative work depending on case load.
17:00–19:00 — variable; sometimes the office, sometimes a walk-and-think route through a six-block radius that takes her past three of her neighborhood contact points.
19:00 onward — depends on case tempo. If quiet: bag work, paperwork, occasional drink at one of two specific bars within a four-block radius. If active: she works the case until she stops.
~01:00 — sleep on the cot.

**Apartment night:** broadly similar but with a longer morning, a real meal cooked at home roughly twice a week (she cooks Trinidadian food her mother taught her; she is competent and unshowy at it), and earlier sleep onset.

**Saturday:** training with Colleen in the morning, errands and personal-business in the afternoon, dinner with Colleen or one of two specific neighborhood friends in the evening, paperwork late.

**Sunday:** the closest she has to a slow day. The Sunday paper from the bodega. Long walk. She is observably less armed on Sundays — sidearm only, not the secondary — and observably more willing to make eye contact with strangers.

---

## 6. Threat Surface, Present

### 6.1 External

She has accumulated, across five decades of operational life, a non-trivial enemies-list. Most are dormant. Several specific categories warrant standing surveillance posture by anyone protecting her:

- Remnant Hand cells with grievance vectors traceable to Colleen.
- Surviving Puppet Master–network assets from the Heroes for Hire collapse.
- A small number of low-grade powered criminals she put away personally who are within parole-window of release.
- Federal interest, low-grade and intermittent, related to her ongoing willingness to take cases adjacent to the enhanced community without registering as an asset of any agency.

She is aware of all of the above. She has hardened her residences, her routes, and her digital footprint to a standard that is not the highest in the street-level community but is high enough that any incursion against her would require dedicated and visible effort.

### 6.2 Internal

The more serious threat surface, in this analyst's view, is internal. The contracted tempo is the first prolonged period of her adult life in which the operational defense has *less to do*. The 3:00 a.m. waking, the upward drift in solitary alcohol, the deferred prosthesis service, and the absence of a named successor for the handler role are all leading indicators of the same underlying pressure. The prognosis stated in the prior workup — *latent long-term cost concentrated in cumulative untreated grief and somatic burden, decompensation if it came presenting as collapse-after-completion* — remains the operative forecast.

The acute risk window is not now. It is the next operational lull after the next significant loss. If Colleen is injured. If Danny is again presumed dead. If a case she has invested in personally ends badly for the missing person on her corkboard. The architecture is built to absorb the loss, finish the related job, and *then* fail. The file should be flagged accordingly.

---

## 7. Where She Is, Right Now

If the question is geographic: in a one-room office above a takeout window in Harlem, or fourteen minutes' walk from it, on any given hour.

If the question is positional: at the late-career inflection point of an operator who has not yet admitted she is at a late-career inflection point. Smaller operation. Denser local roots. Same code. Same arm. Same refusals.

If the question is psychological: holding. Governed. Tired in a way the wisecracks still cover. Self-prescribing the neighborhood and the training partner because the institutional medicine she will not take has a generic version she will. Awake at 4:00 a.m. doing paperwork that does not need doing at 4:00 a.m. Not asking for help. Not yet needing to. Closer to needing to than she has been at any prior point in the file.

She is, in the assessment of this section, exactly where the trajectory predicted she would be — and the next ninety days of her life are the most diagnostic ninety days the file has ever had to read.

— END SECTION —


## Medical History

# MEDICAL HISTORY — SUBJECT: KNIGHT, MERCEDES "MISTY"

*File classification: Somatic Intelligence — longitudinal medical map. Built from on-page evidence, depicted body-mechanics, prosthetic engineering implications, and the diagnostic significance of what canon omits. The omissions are themselves data.*

---

## I. CONSTITUTIONAL BASELINE — PRE-INJURY

Subject presents as a constitutionally robust Black woman, height approximately 5'9", pre-injury weight in the 150–160 lb range carried as athletic muscle with low-normal body fat. The pre-NYPD record is undocumented but the academy and patrol survival profile (and her later sustained capacity to absorb blunt trauma and continue) implies above-average cardiovascular conditioning, well-developed posterior chain, and the bone density typical of someone who lifted, ran, and fought in adolescence. No childhood illness, no congenital condition, no allergy, no surgical history are referenced in any canon. The pre-injury body is functionally a tabula rasa — which is itself diagnostic of how she relates to the medical record: bodies are not *charted* in her cosmology until they break.

Skin: dark brown, photographed in art as evenly pigmented with no visible hypertrophic or keloid scarring in pre-injury depictions — relevant because she is, by ethnic predisposition, *at elevated risk* for keloid formation, and the post-amputation scar bed at the shoulder disarticulation site would, in any realistic medical course, have required steroid injection management or silicone sheet therapy. None of this is on-page. Either Stark-grade reconstruction managed the scar bed surgically at the time of prosthesis integration, or she has lived with a hypertrophic scar shelf at the prosthetic socket she has never spoken about. Both are plausible. Both are characterologically consistent.

Vision and hearing: nothing in the depicted operational record suggests refractive error, and her shooting and driving consistently render at near-elite levels — suggestive of intact 20/20 or corrected-to-normal vision and intact high-frequency hearing pre-blast. Post-blast hearing is a separate question (see §II.C).

Dentition: depicted consistently as intact, even, white — no on-page dental work, no missing teeth despite a career of taking faces from fists. This is implausible without intermittent restorative dentistry she has never narrated.

Menstrual and reproductive baseline pre-injury: undocumented but presumptively normal, given the later confirmed pregnancy.

---

## II. THE INDEX EVENT — BLAST AMPUTATION, RIGHT UPPER EXTREMITY

### A. Mechanism and acute injury

Off-duty, NYPD detective grade, encounters an active improvised explosive in a public space — variously rendered across retellings as a bank, a street, a transit setting. She moves civilians, then physically *shields* the device with her body to direct the blast vector. The device detonates. The right arm is destroyed at or proximal to the shoulder.

The mechanical reality of a body-shielded IED at that proximity is catastrophic:

- **Primary blast injury:** pressure wave through the thoracic cavity. Expected findings — pulmonary contusion, possible tympanic membrane rupture (bilateral, more severe on the right), possible mesenteric bruising. Survival of primary blast at body-contact distance is itself anomalous and implies either a smaller device than the imagery suggests or the kind of statistical luck that becomes part of someone's self-mythology.
- **Secondary blast injury:** fragmentation. The right anterior torso, neck, and jaw would have caught fragments. Inferred on-skin record: a constellation of small puncture scars across the right pectoral, right lateral neck, right mandibular line, and right cheek — small enough to be missed in standard comic art rendering but consistent with a survivor of close-proximity fragmentation.
- **Tertiary blast injury:** displacement. Body thrown. Expected — blunt impact injuries to the contralateral (left) side from landing, possible left clavicular or rib fracture, possible mild traumatic brain injury.
- **Quaternary blast injury:** burn. Right hemithorax and what remained of the proximal shoulder, thermal burn likely 2nd-degree, possibly 3rd-degree at the amputation surface.
- **The amputation itself:** traumatic disarticulation at or near the glenohumeral joint, with avulsion of the brachial plexus root, transection of the axillary artery and vein, and massive acute hemorrhage. Survival to the OR required, at minimum, immediate tourniquet at the axilla or direct vascular compression — almost certainly applied by herself or a bystander before EMS arrival, given proximity to a detonating device.

### B. Acute medical course (inferred — undocumented in canon)

The literature's elision of the convalescence is total. There is no scene of her in a hospital bed. There is no scene of physical therapy. There is no scene of psychiatric consult. The narrative resumes at *she has a new arm and a new job*. From a forensic-medical standpoint the missing course is reconstructable:

- ER stabilization, massive transfusion protocol, surgical debridement of the stump and vascular control. 
- ICU course minimum two weeks: ventilator support given pulmonary contusion, sepsis watch given burn and contamination from blast debris.
- Step-down and surgical revision: at shoulder disarticulation level, the surgical stump is typically revised multiple times to produce a clean closure over the scapula and remaining clavicle/acromion. In her case, given subsequent prosthetic socket integration at the scapulothoracic region, the revision was probably more aggressive — retention of the acromion and clavicle as anchor points for a Stark-engineered osseointegrated mount.
- Rehabilitation: minimum 6–12 months for a baseline below-shoulder amputee; longer with cybernetic neural interface integration. Inferred: she did this work in private, quickly, ungrudgingly, and refused to be visited by anyone other than Colleen Wing.

### C. Sequelae from the blast itself, distinct from the limb loss

- **Tinnitus, right-dominant.** Inferred from blast proximity. Never on-page acknowledged. Her habit, observable in art across decades, of cocking her head to favor the left ear in quiet rooms is consistent.
- **Mild high-frequency hearing loss, right ear.** Operationally compensated by training herself to scan rooms left-side leading.
- **Microscarring across right anterior chest, neck, jaw line.** Cosmetically reduced by Stark-era surgical revision; never to her noted distress.
- **Possible mild post-concussive sequelae** in the first post-blast year — headache, photosensitivity, irritability — fully resolved or fully suppressed by the time the published record resumes.

### D. Psychological impact of the index event

The pivotal datum: she does not grieve the arm. She does not grieve the body. She accepts the prosthesis, refuses the desk, and quits the institution that offered her diminishment. The injury becomes the founding event of an *identity* (the PI, the operator, the handler) rather than of a *wound*. This is the most psychologically expensive choice in her chart — not because it was wrong, but because the unspent grief did not disappear; it was banked. The interest accrues across decades and is paid in §V (reproductive loss), §VI (chronic pain), and §VII (alcohol).

---

## III. THE PROSTHESIS — DEVICE, INTEGRATION, AND CHRONIC LOAD

### A. Engineering profile

The original Stark-built bionic right arm is, on its face, a triumph: full-length replacement from shoulder disarticulation socket through scapular and clavicular anchorage to articulated fingertips, polished chrome/steel finish with no cosmetic skin cover (a deliberate choice — she does not hide it). Functional capacities documented across canon include:

- Superhuman grip and crush strength localized to the limb (canonical demonstrations include bending firearm slides, crushing pistol barrels, denting steel doors).
- Reinforced impact tolerance — she uses the limb as a shield and as a striking weapon.
- Variable run-to-run integrated capacities: EMP discharge, concussive force emitter, magnetic adherence, occasional tooling.
- Neural interface fidelity sufficient for fine motor task at near-organic resolution (she shoots two-handed with no degradation, manipulates locks, types).

### B. The kinetic asymmetry — the chronic medical problem nobody dramatizes

The prosthesis is *augmented*. Her skeleton is not. Every time she delivers a prosthetic punch at full output, the reaction force travels through:

1. Prosthetic socket → scapulothoracic mount → her organic clavicle, scapula, and ribcage.
2. From the scapula through the spine, particularly cervical (C5–C7) and upper thoracic (T1–T4) segments.
3. From the spine through the pelvic girdle into the legs.

Expected and inferable chronic findings, cumulative across the published career:

- **Right scapulothoracic and clavicular chronic pain.** Persistent, exacerbated in cold weather, in the rain, after high-load engagements. She rubs her right shoulder unconsciously when seated.
- **Cervical spondylosis, early-onset, C5–C7.** Inferred from the head-carriage in modern-era art (slight forward head posture, particularly when tired). Probable referred pain into the right posterior neck and occipital region. Episodic tension-type headaches.
- **Compensatory left-side overuse syndrome.** Because the prosthesis is, paradoxically, *too strong* for many fine-motor tasks (cooking, writing, applying makeup, handling a coffee cup), she has shifted into left-hand dominance for nearly all non-combat activity. The result: left rotator cuff impingement risk, left lateral epicondylitis (tennis elbow) episodes she would write off as soreness, possible left thumb CMC joint arthritis emerging in her late 30s.
- **Phantom limb sensation.** Universal in major-limb amputees, present even with sophisticated prosthesis. Inferable: episodic itch, cramp, or position-sensation referred to the absent biological arm, particularly at night when the prosthesis is doffed. She has never spoken of it on-page. She almost certainly experiences it nightly.
- **Socket dermatitis at the integration site.** The skin under any prosthetic socket sustains mechanical and thermal stress and is prone to contact dermatitis, folliculitis, and recurrent low-grade infection. Stark-grade interface materials mitigate this; do not eliminate it.
- **Postural drift.** Right shoulder carried fractionally lower in art across the modern era — the prosthesis is heavier than the organic limb it replaced. Pelvic tilt, mild compensatory thoracolumbar scoliosis (rightward convex) emerging.
- **Cold and EM weather sensitivity.** Metallic prosthesis loses or gains heat faster than organic tissue. Inferred — she avoids prolonged exposure to deep cold, wears the prosthesis under sleeve in winter not for concealment but for thermal regulation.

### C. Maintenance and service — the catastrophic absence

A Stark-grade neural-integrated limb would require, at minimum: monthly software/firmware updates, quarterly mechanical service, annual full diagnostic, and lifetime monitoring of the neural interface for impedance drift, scar encapsulation around electrode arrays, and biofouling. None of this is depicted. She is never on-page in a service appointment. The inference is one of three: (i) Rand and successor engineers do house calls — plausible; (ii) she handles routine maintenance herself, having learned the system — plausible and characterologically consistent; (iii) she defers service longer than she should and the limb periodically degrades — most plausible, and consistent with the same pattern that defers her own medical care.

### D. Psychological integration of the prosthesis

This is, paradoxically, the *healthiest* somatic relationship in her chart. She does not hide the arm. She does not cover it with synthetic skin. She does not name it. She does not apologize for it. She allows it to be seen, allows it to be a tell, allows people to register it and recalibrate. The prosthesis is *self*. This integration is genuinely successful and is the one major counterargument to a global reading of somatic dissociation — she has dissociated from the *loss*, not from the *limb*. The limb is owned. The loss is unmentioned. The distinction is clinically important: she has built an identity that incorporates the device, which is adaptive; she has refused the mourning the device replaced, which is not.

---

## IV. CAREER-ACCUMULATED TRAUMA — THE OPERATIONAL CHART

Across approximately fifteen on-page years of street-level operational work (canonical compression of nearly fifty years of publication), the cumulative blunt and penetrating trauma load is large. Reconstructed inventory:

- **Gunshot wounds:** multiple. At minimum two documented on-page graze or through-and-through wounds (thigh, flank). Likely additional minor wounds compressed by narrative. No documented major vascular or visceral injury post-amputation. Each event would have required ER evaluation; she has likely treated several at home or with a cooperative practitioner who does not ask questions.
- **Blunt-force injuries:** routine. Contusions, lacerations, the occasional rib fracture (consistent with the way she leads with her body into engagements). Inferred: at least one healed rib fracture set without medical attention; chronic costochondral tenderness on the right.
- **Knife wounds:** at minimum two depicted — defensive lacerations to the left forearm (the limb she now uses to parry, because the prosthesis catches and breaks blades but the organic arm absorbs them), and a torso wound during a *Daughters of the Dragon* engagement.
- **Concussion(s):** at minimum three to five inferred across career. Cumulative subclinical CTE risk is non-trivial and would not present clinically for another decade or more.
- **Burns:** beyond the index event, episodic small thermal and chemical burns occupationally acquired.
- **Smoke inhalation:** several episodes consistent with fire-and-explosion case work.
- **Sexual assault, attempted or threatened:** depicted in at least one bounty-hunting engagement; resolved violently by her. Not subsequently processed on-page.

The body she carries into her late 30s is a body that has been used hard and serviced little.

---

## V. REPRODUCTIVE HISTORY — THE UNSPOKEN CHAPTER

The most psychologically dense entry in the medical chart. During the *Daughters of the Dragon* arc, she becomes pregnant — partner contextually Danny Rand, given the timeframe — and *conceals* the pregnancy from:

- the father,
- her work partner (Colleen Wing),
- her presumed medical providers,
- the reader, until mid-arc disclosure.

She continues to take bounty work and engage in physical combat through the pregnancy. She miscarries during a combat engagement, on-panel, in a way the script frames as both medical event and metaphor.

The medical reality is severe. Mid-pregnancy loss under blunt or penetrating combat trauma is a hemorrhagic emergency. Depending on gestational age:

- First trimester loss: heavy bleeding, possible D&C requirement, RhoGAM if Rh-negative, post-loss monitoring for retained products.
- Second trimester loss: surgical evacuation almost certain, longer recovery, higher infection risk, hormonally significant lactation suppression needs.

None of this aftercare is depicted. The next time we see her, she is upright, dressed, working.

The concealment is the diagnostic event, not the loss itself. Concealing a pregnancy from one's primary partner *and one's medical providers* is not absentmindedness; it is a defensive structure. The implicit logic reconstructs as: *if I name this, it will be taken from me — either the pregnancy will take the work from me, or the work will take the pregnancy from me — and I cannot allow either party to make that choice for me.* She kept both, until the body chose. After the choice was made for her, she returned to the architecture that had not failed: work.

Psychological impact: profound and largely unmetabolized. This is the wound the prosthesis cannot route around. The arm could be replaced; the pregnancy could not. The somatic dissociation that served her for the limb loss was applied to the reproductive loss with markedly worse results — because here there was a *grief object* (a not-yet-child, a possible future) that the defensive architecture had no script for. She has not, in subsequent canon, been depicted seeking another pregnancy, ruling one out, discussing it with Danny, or processing the loss with Colleen. The silence is the symptom.

Secondary medical considerations: post-loss hormonal disruption, possible secondary amenorrhea for some months, possible mood disturbance attributed (by her) to case stress rather than to the loss. Long-term fertility status: undocumented and unexplored by her on-page.

---

## VI. CHRONIC PAIN PROFILE

Synthesized from the above:

- **Right shoulder/scapulothoracic:** daily low-grade ache, episodic acute spikes after high-load prosthetic use.
- **Cervical (C5–C7), right-dominant:** daily stiffness, weekly tension-type headache.
- **Left rotator cuff / left lateral elbow:** episodic overuse pain.
- **Thoracolumbar, right paraspinal:** postural strain, worse after long driving or stakeout sitting.
- **Right hemithorax (costochondral):** intermittent, weather-sensitive.
- **Phantom limb sensation:** nocturnal, ungraded by her, untreated.
- **Tension headache, occipital:** weekly to daily under operational tempo.

Pharmacologic management: over-the-counter NSAIDs (inferred — ibuprofen, naproxen), used routinely, almost certainly at long-term doses that elevate gastric and renal risk. She is not on a chronic opioid regimen. She is not on a documented muscle relaxant. She self-medicates with alcohol (§VII) and with hot showers, deep heat, and the kind of stretching she learned from Colleen, who learned it from her father.

She has never, in any depicted scene, asked anyone for pain medication, pain management referral, or rehabilitation. This is the single most consistent medical-behavioral pattern in the file.

---

## VII. SUBSTANCE USE

**Alcohol.** Moderate to upper-moderate by quantity, characterologically reliable by pattern. Drink of preference: brown liquor neat or on a single rock — bourbon when available, whiskey otherwise. Beer in social settings. Wine rarely. Pattern:

- Social with Colleen, two to four drinks, weekly.
- Post-case solitary, one to three drinks, situational.
- Operational dry — she does not drink before or during active casework.

The line between affect-regulation and at-risk use is thin and the canon understates it. The clinical concern is not *current* use; it is *trajectory*. Under sustained loss (Danny, Colleen, the loss of the handler role), the use would predictably escalate. She is the constitution that drinks more, not less, under grief.

**Tobacco.** Episodic. Probably a social smoker — bummed cigarettes at bars, on stakeouts — never a daily habit. Generationally and occupationally plausible.

**Caffeine.** High and continuous. Black coffee, large, frequent. Operational tempo runs on it. Probable mild chronic caffeine dependence with rebound headache on withdrawal.

**Cannabis.** Plausible occasional use socially; no operational impact.

**Stimulants, opioids, sedatives:** not depicted, not characterologically consistent.

**Other:** no documented pharmaceutical regimen, no contraceptive method on-page, no antidepressant or anxiolytic. The absence of standard primary care is itself a finding.

---

## VIII. SLEEP, NUTRITION, PREVENTIVE CARE

**Sleep.** Irregular, operationally driven, short. Inferred 5–6 hours on working nights, with attempted recovery sleep on off-days that is itself disrupted by phantom limb sensation, shoulder pain, and probable hyperarousal residue. Sleeps with a firearm within reach. Does not share a bed easily; the prosthesis is doffed at night, and the doffing is a private act.

**Nutrition.** Functional, not optimized. High caffeine, moderate protein, irregular meals scheduled around casework. Probably underhydrated. Iron status worth checking given prior hemorrhagic events and reproductive history.

**Preventive care.** Effectively absent. No on-page primary care provider, no documented gynecologic care post-miscarriage, no documented dental care, no documented mental health care. The prosthesis is the one body system that arguably gets attention, and even that is informal.

**Mental health care.** None documented. Defensible operational reasons (confidentiality, threat exposure of providers); insufficient on the actual clinical need.

---

## IX. INTEGRATED SOMATIC ASSESSMENT

The body she inhabits in her late 30s is the body of an operator who has survived everything asked of her and accounted for none of it. The prosthesis is integrated; the loss is not. The chronic pain is real; the pain narrative is not. The reproductive loss is foundational; the reproductive aftercare is invisible. The substance pattern is currently functional; the trajectory is risk-bearing. The sleep is poor; the hypervigilance that disrupts it is reframed as professionalism. The preventive care is absent; the constitution has, so far, made absence affordable.

Prognosis, somatic: she has another ten to fifteen years of current operational tempo before the chronic load — cervical, scapular, gastric, renal, and accumulated subclinical concussion — begins to compound visibly. Prognosis, psychiatric-somatic interface: the first major somatic decompensation will not be musculoskeletal; it will be the first night she cannot work and cannot drink past the unprocessed material the work and the drink have been holding. That night is on the schedule. It has not been scheduled.

— END MEDICAL HISTORY —


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS — KNIGHT, MERCEDES "MISTY"

*Compiled from longitudinal observation, canonical visual record, and inferred extrapolation from documented behavior. The body is the truthful witness; the subject's verbal record is, by her own architecture, partial.*

---

## I. STANDING ARCHITECTURE — THE BASELINE FRAME

The subject carries 5'9" of athletic-build mass in a posture that has been quietly deformed by asymmetric augmentation for the entirety of her post-injury adult life. **Baseline standing posture:** weight loaded approximately 55/45 onto the left (organic) leg, with the prosthetic shoulder riding two to four degrees higher than the organic shoulder — the prosthesis is heavier than meat and gravity has been pulling the contralateral thoracic erectors into chronic compensation for decades. The right scapula sits in slight elevation and forward roll; the left scapula has migrated into mild retraction to counterbalance. Across published renderings the head sits over the body in a barely-perceptible left-of-center carriage. She does not know she does this.

**Hands in repose.** Organic left hand rests with the thumb folded across the index finger — a residual self-soothe that predates the injury (inferable from its pre-augmentation universality in early-career depictions). The chrome right hand defaults to a relaxed half-curl with the index finger marginally extended, as if always one beat from a trigger pull or a point. When she is genuinely calm — Colleen's apartment, late, off-shift — the bionic fingers go fully slack and audibly tick faintly against whatever surface they touch as the actuators idle.

**Hip set.** Right hip cocked forward when standing in conversation, which reads on the street as attitude and is in fact the path-of-least-strain stance for a body that has rebalanced around a steel shoulder. The hip-cock is more pronounced when the conversation is adversarial; in genuine threat it disappears and the hips square to the target.

---

## II. GAIT

**Calm-state walk.** A four-beat heel-toe with mild swagger from the hip rather than the shoulder. The arms do not swing symmetrically — the organic left arm swings a clean natural arc, the bionic right arm swings perhaps sixty percent of that amplitude. The prosthetic mass is too heavy for full passive swing and the subject has unconsciously dampened it; she carries the chrome arm as one carries a holstered weapon, with awareness of its inertia.

**Working walk.** Heel strike sharpens. Stride shortens by perhaps four inches. Eyes do the room sweep — left-center-right-up-behind in a pattern so habituated it survives intoxication. She walks the inside of a sidewalk by preference (wall side, not curb), reverses to curb side when expecting vehicular threat.

**Pursuit gait.** Forward lean from the ankle, not the waist. The bionic arm comes up to chest height and stays there as a counterbalanced battering instrument; the organic arm pumps. She is faster than she should be at her augmentation-adjusted weight because she runs from clean hip extension — NYPD academy mechanics, never lost.

**Tired walk.** End of a long case, after midnight: the prosthetic shoulder visibly drops. She rolls it back into position roughly every fortieth step, an unconscious tic. The left hand finds a pocket. The swagger flattens into something closer to a trudge that she would deny if observed.

---

## III. THE FACE

**Eyes.** Dark brown, deep-set, with a working-investigator's slow blink rate at baseline (roughly 12–14/minute, below population average — she is a watcher). Pupil-tracking is lateral-dominant; she clocks peripheries before centers. The microexpression that precedes a verbal sharp comeback is a single raised left eyebrow and a half-millimeter compression of the lower lip — visible to Colleen, invisible to most subjects of the comeback.

**Mouth.** Resting expression carries a faint downward set at the corners that reads as skepticism. The smile, when offered, is asymmetric — left corner rises first and higher, the right lags by perhaps a tenth of a second. Full open-mouth laughter is rare and concentrated almost entirely in Colleen's company; in mixed company she laughs through the nose with the mouth closed.

**Jaw.** Holds tension at the masseter. Probable nocturnal bruxism — the jawline carries the slight hypertrophy consistent with years of clenching. Under interrogation pressure or grief, the jaw sets and the chin lifts a quarter inch; this is the closest she comes to a public tell of distress.

**The Look.** The detective stare — chin slightly lowered, eyes held on the subject's eyes without blink for three to five seconds longer than social convention allows — is a deliberate deployable. She uses it on suspects, on landlords, on Danny when he is dissociating, on the doctor she will not see.

---

## IV. THE HAIR

The afro is signature, maintained, and operationally legible. **Maintenance ritual:** weekly deep wash, picking out in front of a bathroom mirror with a wide-tooth afro pick held in the *left* hand — she will not bring the chrome fingers near her scalp, the asymmetry there is the only somatic site where she behaves as if the prosthesis is not fully her own. Reshaping by hand-pat in a circumferential pattern that she completes in roughly forty seconds before leaving any mirror.

**State indicator.** When fully tended, the afro is symmetric and high; when she has been working a case for more than seventy-two hours, it asymmetrizes — flattened on whichever side she has been sleeping on in the office chair. Colleen reads case duration off her hair before she reads it off her face. In genuine grief or post-failure crash, the hair goes uncombed for days and she pulls a scarf or watch cap over it rather than fix it — the only public concession she ever makes to interior collapse.

---

## V. THE HANDS AND THE ARM

The two hands have separate behavioral repertoires and this is the most psychologically dense fact in the somatic file.

**The organic left hand** does fine motor, intimate touch, eating, the pick through the hair, the cigarette if she's having one (occasional, social), the keyboard typing in clusters punctuated by the right index hunting a single key at a time, the touch to another person's face or forearm, the trigger pull on her sidearm by preference when accuracy matters.

**The chrome right hand** does force, threat display, door-opening, weapon-disarming, the lifting of furniture, the bracing punch into a wall when frustrated, the holding-down of a struggling subject. It also does the resting-on-the-bar gesture that makes whoever is next to her at the bar choose to move one stool over. She is aware of this and uses it.

**The hand never touches her own face.** Across the canonical visual record there is no instance of the bionic fingers contacting her cheek, mouth, eye, scalp, or throat. She scratches an itch on her face with the left hand even when the right is closer. This is the somatic shibboleth of the dissociation — the prosthesis is integrated as *self-acting-on-world* but resisted as *self-acting-on-self*. The arm is an instrument; her face is hers.

**Sound profile of the arm.** Faint servo whine at full extension; a low harmonic hum when bearing load; an audible clack against hard surfaces that she has stopped registering and others have not. In silence she sometimes flexes the fingers to make the sound, as one drums fingers — a self-stimulating tic she does not know she has.

---

## VI. GESTURE LEXICON

- **Two-finger point** (left index and middle, together): direction-giving, suspect-indicating, the *you* in an argument. Cop residue.
- **Open-palm-down press** (left hand): de-escalation, used on Luke when he's reaching the line, on Danny mid-dissociation.
- **Bionic forefinger tap on a tabletop**: thinking gesture, metronomic, three to five taps then a pause then three to five more. Increases in tempo with frustration.
- **Both-hands-on-hips**: the cop stance, deployed when she wants the room to know she's in charge. The bionic hand on the right hip is the more aggressive posture; she knows.
- **Bionic shoulder roll**: discomfort tell, the one she cannot suppress. Once per long conversation, twice if seated too long, continuously if the interface is acting up.
- **Left hand to back of neck**: the *I cannot say this* gesture, rare, observed only with Colleen and once with Danny on the night before his second presumed death.
- **Chin jerk upward** as greeting to known associates; full nod for civilians; no acknowledgment for adversaries until she speaks.

---

## VII. SLEEP ARCHITECTURE

**Total nightly sleep:** 4.5 to 6 hours on a working week, 7 to 8 on the rare flat week. Sleep onset latency is *fast* (under ten minutes) when she lies down — a workaholic's gift — but she does not lie down until she has run a perimeter pattern: window check, door bolt, sidearm placement on the nightstand within left-arm reach, bionic arm resting prosthesis-side-up on the mattress beside her (never under the body — pressure on the interface is uncomfortable and she has learned).

**Sleep position:** left lateral recumbent, organic side down, prosthetic arm draped across the body or extended forward. She does not sleep on her right side. She does not sleep supine for more than the first twenty minutes.

**Wake pattern:** sleeps through ambient city noise that would wake civilians (sirens, traffic, neighbor doors) and wakes instantly at proximate sounds (footstep in her hallway, key in a lock not hers, the specific creak of her own apartment's third floorboard from the door). Wakes with the left hand already moving toward the sidearm before the eyes open. This is post-injury hardwiring.

**Nightmares.** Not depicted on-page; inferred to exist by the subsyndromal PTSD read. Probable content domain: blast/auditory, not visual — sustained low-grade startle response to sudden loud noises is observable across the canon. If she dreams them she does not report them. Colleen has, in her own published narration, mentioned waking to find the subject sitting at the kitchen table at 4 a.m. with the light on, cleaning a pistol she has already cleaned.

---

## VIII. EATING

**Tempo:** fast eater, fork in left hand European-style without realizing it (the bionic right does not handle silverware against ceramic well — the feedback is wrong — and she has migrated her dominant eating hand). Coffee precedes food; food precedes water.

**Diet:** street-grade. Bodega coffee, deli sandwiches, the diner two blocks from Knightwing where the waitress knows the order. Late dinners, often standing at a counter. Notable absence of cooking-for-self in the canonical record despite competent cooking-for-others when Danny or Luke is at the apartment — feeding others is care, feeding self is fuel.

**Hydration:** chronically low. Coffee and beer do most of the work. The headaches she does not mention are probably partly this.

**Drinking pattern.** Beer in company (preference: domestic, longneck, peeled label — she peels the label with her left thumb in a slow methodical strip). Whiskey alone, neat, two fingers, sipped slowly across forty minutes. The shift from beer to whiskey is the state-change marker; Colleen has tracked it for years.

---

## IX. SEXUAL AND INTIMATE SOMATICS

The intimate register is rationed, deliberate, and somatically asymmetric.

**Touch initiation.** With Danny, with whoever the partner of the era is: the first touch is almost always the left hand — to the jaw, to the forearm, to the back of the neck. The right comes later, and lands on neutral territory (shoulder, hip, back) rather than on face or genitals. The somatic dissociation around the prosthesis-as-intimate-instrument persists; she has not resolved it and there is no evidence she has tried.

**Received touch.** She does not flinch from being touched on the prosthesis, but she does not lean into it either. Touch on the organic shoulder, the neck, the small of the back is received with audible exhale. Touch on the prosthetic shoulder reads as touch on a coat — acknowledged, not felt-as-self.

**Postcoital pattern** (inferable from depicted morning scenes with Danny): she is the one who gets up first. The body that has just been intimate is reabsorbed into the operating body within minutes. She makes coffee. She checks the window. The intimacy is real and it is also finite.

**Kissing register.** Brief, firm, frequently in greeting or farewell rather than as sustained sensual act. The long kiss is reserved for the rare on-page moments of acknowledged-fragility — Danny returning from presumed death, the night before a known-dangerous op. She is not undemonstrative; she is *economical*.

---

## X. PAIN BEHAVIOR

The pain inventory is large and the expression repertoire is tiny.

- **Shoulder/clavicular ache** (prosthesis-side chronic): rolled out unconsciously with the shoulder-roll tic, never named.
- **Cervical strain** (compensation): managed by pressing the back of the skull into the headrest of any chair tall enough for it. Probable underlying tension headaches.
- **Phantom limb sensation**: undepicted, almost certainly present, possibly resolved-by-replacement (prosthesis-as-rich-sensory-input can damp phantom in the literature). If present, she does not say.
- **Acute injury (combat-incurred):** she walks it off. The face does not change. The voice does not change. The walk does change — minutely, observable to Colleen, to no one else. She will accept a wound being treated by Colleen with no verbal acknowledgment beyond *thanks*; she will refuse treatment from anyone she has not slept beside or worked beside for years.

---

## XI. GROOMING AND DRESS

Practical, considered, and uniform-coded. Leather jacket (multiple, rotated by season and operational need; the heaviest is also the most armored — she has had a tailor sew kevlar paneling into the lining and would deny it). Fitted tactical or street streetwear underneath. Boots with a low heel, soled for grip, broken in over months before they enter rotation. Holster on the left hip (cross-draw to organic hand). Backup at the right ankle.

**Jewelry:** minimal. A pair of small gold hoops, present across decades — these survive scenes the rest of her clothing does not. They are not decorative; they are continuity. Inference: pre-injury possessions, possibly from her mother.

**Scent profile:** soap, gun oil, leather, occasional cigarette smoke from being in rooms with smokers, the faint metallic tang of the prosthesis's lubrication cycle. No perfume. The absence is intentional — perfume is identifiable in dark rooms.

---

## XII. STATE-SHIFTED SOMATIC PROFILES

**Calm (with Colleen, off-shift, apartment).** Shoulders drop. Hair tended. Bionic fingers slack and ticking idly. Mouth softens. Laughter present. Left hand finds tea or beer. Posture loose; she will actually sit back into a couch. The body she does not show anyone else.

**Working (case-active, baseline).** Posture squared. Eye sweep continuous. Gait shortened. Wisecrack frequency up. Coffee continuous. Bionic forefinger taps when thinking. This is the public face; this is what almost every witness across her career has seen.

**Stressed (case stalled, sleep-deprived, deadline).** Jaw sets. Shoulder rolls increase to every few minutes. Hair asymmetrizes. Beer migrates to whiskey. Verbal sharpness escalates into actual cutting. Touch tolerance drops — she will pull back from a hand on the prosthetic shoulder she would have ignored a day earlier.

**Threatened (active danger, immediate).** Hips square to threat. Bionic arm rises to chest center-line. Organic hand goes to sidearm or to the line of the sidearm. Breathing drops to deep diaphragmatic — she trained this and it stuck. Voice drops half an octave and slows. The wisecracks vanish. She becomes, somatically, very still — and this is the most dangerous version of her body.

**Intimate (rare, with trusted partner).** Left hand initiates. Right hand stays on neutral ground. Eyes hold longer. Voice softens to a register no operational counterpart has heard. Postcoital reabsorption into operating body is fast but not cold. She will sleep more deeply beside one specific person than she sleeps alone.

**Grieving (post-loss, post-failure).** Terse. Movements economical to the point of stillness. Hair untended, often covered. Whiskey solitary. Long sits at the kitchen table with the light on. She will not cry where she can be seen. Whether she cries where she cannot is not in the record; the somatic evidence — puffy eye tissue in next-day appearances, voice slightly roughened — suggests she does, briefly, and then washes her face and goes back to work.

---

*The body keeps the file the subject will not keep. Every shoulder roll is a page of the unwritten medical chart; every untouched cheek is a sentence of the unspoken grief log; every bionic tap on a tabletop is a metronome counting the unprocessed seconds between the blast and now. She is, somatically, one of the most coherent operators in the street-level theater — and the coherence is held together by a thousand small economies, each of which is itself a wound's signature.*

— END SOMATIC ATLAS —


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS — KNIGHT, MERCEDES "MISTY"

## 1. Baseline Style: Earned-Secure With Avoidant Deactivation Under Threat

The subject does not present as a classic insecure attachment type, and the file should resist that easy read. Across roughly fifty in-universe years of documented relational behavior, she demonstrates the load-bearing features of **earned security**: she can sustain a single primary intimate bond (Colleen Wing) for decades without rupture; she tolerates conflict without abandonment terror; she does not test partners; she does not punish absence; she returns calls; she keeps her word; she does not engineer crises to extract reassurance. These are the negatives — the things insecurely-attached operators do that she conspicuously does not do — and they are diagnostically louder than the positives.

What overlays the secure baseline is a clean, almost textbook **avoidant deactivation** that switches on under two specific stressors: (a) acute loss of a loved figure, and (b) any solicitation of her own vulnerability. Under either condition she goes terse, redirects to task, refuses offered care, and resumes operational tempo within hours of an event that would lay out a less defended person for weeks. This is not flatness. It is a learned valve. Watch her shoulders when someone tries to comfort her after a hit — the prosthetic side rises a quarter-inch, the organic side stays level; she does not consciously know she does this.

The origin of the secure baseline must be inferred — childhood is canonically thin — but the inference is well-supported. Securely-built children become adults who can run Knightwing Restorations as a co-equal partnership for decades; insecurely-built ones cannot. Somewhere in the Knight household in pre-NYPD Harlem there was a caregiver, almost certainly female and probably maternal or grand-maternal, who delivered consistent, contingent responsiveness. The deactivation layer is overwhelmingly **acquired**: imposed by (i) the 1970s NYPD environment, which selected ruthlessly for armored Black women, and (ii) the blast injury, which welded the armor permanently in place at the precise developmental window — young adulthood — when intimate templates are still being negotiated.

## 2. The Colleen Wing Bond: The Control Variable

Every relational pattern in this file must be read against the Colleen Wing dyad, because it is the **only relationship in which Knight's defenses are fully off-line**, and it therefore reveals what she is capable of when she permits herself.

The bond is fused without being enmeshed. They share business equity, residence in multiple eras, operational risk, weapons inventory, and a private vocabulary. They share post-mission silence — the file notes that on returning to the office after a violent case, neither speaks for the first eight to twelve minutes; one makes coffee, the other cleans a weapon; the protocol is wordless. They have argued on-page, repeatedly, including over each other's romantic choices, and the arguments do not threaten the bond. They have physically cared for each other's bodies — wound dressing, sobering-up, hair, the prosthetic's manual service in field conditions when Knight will not see a Stark tech — without sexual or romantic charge and without the discomfort that would attend such care between most adult women not raised together.

The Colleen bond functions as the subject's **single regulatory anchor**. When it is stable, the avoidant deactivation is dormant and she is the warm, wry, generous operator the 1970s books depict. When it is threatened — Colleen in danger, Colleen's substance arcs, Colleen briefly displaced by a partner of her own — Knight's affect tightens measurably. The Colleen channel is the one pathway through which she can be told something true about herself and accept it. Praise from Danny is received as romance-script and discounted; praise from Luke is received as collegiality; praise from Colleen lands. This is the only voice in her interior that is not screened.

**Operational implication:** Colleen Wing is the single most consequential person in the subject's threat surface. Her death or compromise would not produce a borderline collapse — Knight does not have that architecture — but would produce a slow, months-long erosion of the avoidant defenses' efficiency, with cumulative untreated material surfacing in the form of dreams, somatic symptoms, and progressively narrower social contact. She would finish her cases. Then she would not take new ones.

## 3. Romantic Pattern: The Stable Party to a Variable Other

Across the romantic record — primary: Daniel Rand, long arc; secondary: Samuel Wilson, intermittent; tertiary and incidental: various — the structural signature is invariant. **She selects partners whose damage exceeds hers and whose extraordinary capacity licenses her caretaking as collaboration rather than nursing.** Rand is dissociative, mystically-displaced, periodically dead, raised by monks, structurally incapable of running a household; Wilson is a trauma-saturated combatant carrying public-figure weight. Neither is a man who could sit across a breakfast table and ask her how she actually is. This is the point.

Within these relationships her pattern is rigorously consistent:

- **She does the logistics.** Meals, scheduling, rent, legal, the calls to people who are angry at him, the bail. Across the Claremont/Byrne run this is shown granularly: she is the one who tells Danny when to eat, who books the flights, who fields Joy Meachum.
- **She supplies physical courage.** She is in front of the partner in every doorway, every initial assault, every breach. The bionic arm is consistently the lead element entering a room.
- **She rations disclosure.** The interior content she shares with Colleen — fear, the arm, the pregnancy — is *not* shared with Danny in any depicted scene. He learns of the miscarriage through circumstance, not from her. This is the single most diagnostic data point in her romantic record.
- **She does not protest absence.** When Danny disappears to K'un L'un, when he dies, when he is replaced by a Skrull — she does not pursue, she does not call mutual friends in grief, she does not write to him in her head on-page. She works. When he returns she resumes without ceremony and without an audited reckoning.
- **She does not test.** No staged jealousies, no withdrawn affection-as-bait, no ultimatums. Partnership is delivered at a constant rate; her interior is held at a constant distance.

This is **caretaker-as-armor**: the giving of practical love at high volume *is itself* the wall behind which the disclosing self stays. A partner can receive limitless competent care from her and still never know what frightens her. Rand, after roughly forty years of intermittent partnership, almost certainly does not know. Wilson does not. Cage — never a lover, always a brother-figure — knows more than either by virtue of standing closer to Colleen.

Sexual intimacy in the depicted record reads as confident, present, and unstrained. There is no shame architecture around the body in *sexual* contexts; the somatic dissociation operates in *medical* and *reproductive* contexts specifically. She is comfortable being desired. She is uncomfortable being examined.

## 4. The Damaged-Men Cluster: Luke Cage, Daniel Rand, Others

The protective stance toward damaged high-capacity men extends beyond romance. With Cage in his early Seagate-trauma years she occupies a sibling-cum-handler role: she translates him to outsiders, screens his contacts, intervenes when his temper jeopardizes a case. With Sam Wilson in crossover appearances she defaults to operational backstop. With Paladin, with Shang-Chi in passing, with Iron Fist's circle of broken martial-arts orphans — she is the woman who organizes the room and tells the men what to do next, and the men comply, and this is welcomed by both sides.

The pattern's psychological function is twofold. It is **genuinely generative** — these men are more functional in her vicinity than out of it, and she knows this and takes pride in it appropriately, without grandiosity. It is also **defensively useful** — being the stable one in the room means no one in the room is asking her to be unstable. A woman surrounded by men whose damage is louder than hers will never be asked to address her own.

She is, accordingly, **markedly less generative around women operators of comparable capacity**. With Jessica Jones she is correct but cool. With Elektra, during the Heroes for Hire handler run, she is professional and slightly competitive. With Monica Rambeau, Storm in crossover, Carol Danvers — courteous, never close. The fused intimacy with Colleen is not a template she extends; it is a sui generis exception. Other women would see her, and being seen is not what she has structured her life to receive.

## 5. Trust Architecture: Earned in Foxholes, Forfeited Once

Trust is granted in a specific currency: **demonstrated competence under fire** plus **demonstrated discretion about her interior**. People who try to earn her trust through warmth, gifts, or stated affection score low. People who do the work without performing about it score high. This is why Cage was inside the wall within months of meeting her and why far more emotionally articulate operators have never crossed it.

Betrayal is processed by **single-event revocation followed by behavioral correctness**. When the Heroes for Hire operation collapses under Puppet Master manipulation she does not stage a confrontation, does not nurse a feud, does not require apology — she withdraws the operational stack, recodes the relationship to arm's-length, and continues to be civilly professional with the betrayer in subsequent encounters. She does not, however, restore. The revocation is permanent and quiet. The file should note this: she is not a grudge-keeper in any visible sense, and she is therefore systematically misread as forgiving. She is not forgiving. She has simply downgraded you and not told you.

The exception, again, is Colleen. Colleen has repeatedly done things — in her substance arcs, in the Hand-affiliation arcs — that from anyone else would trigger silent revocation. From Colleen they trigger intervention, argument, and forgiveness. The Colleen channel does not downgrade.

## 6. The Repair Mechanism

Knight repairs ruptures through **action, not language**. After conflict she will reappear with coffee, with a case lead, with an offer of backup; she will not deliver an apology in words and she will not solicit one. The repair is implicit and proven by behavior over the following days. This works adequately within her existing circle, who speak the same dialect; it fails systematically with partners who require verbal repair, and contributes to the slow attenuation of several of her secondary relationships across the decades.

She is capable of apology — there are isolated scenes — but the apologies are clipped, present-tense, and immediately followed by a redirect to task. "I shouldn't have. We need to move." She does not stay in the apology. Staying in the apology would mean sitting inside her own wrongness with someone watching, and that is one of the two or three things she will not do.

## 7. Dependency: The Asymmetry She Will Accept

She permits dependency in one direction only: **others may depend on her without limit; she depends on others operationally but not emotionally**. She will accept tactical support, intel, a ride, money fronted on a case, a safehouse. She will not accept comfort, reassurance, or care for her body absent overwhelming necessity. Offered a shoulder to cry on she will deflect; offered a weapon she needs she will accept and thank you crisply.

The one zone where she accepts emotional dependency — receiving, not giving — is, predictably, with Colleen, and even there it is rationed and reciprocal. They do not lean on each other simultaneously; one is always the stable one. The shift between roles is wordless and tracked by both.

## 8. The Relational Template, Stated Plainly

Across every dyad — romantic, fraternal, professional, adversarial — the underlying template is the same:

> *I will see you accurately and quickly. I will stand in front of you in the doorway. I will handle the logistics of your life and your crisis. I will not ask you to handle mine. I will not tell you what mine is. If you betray me I will continue to be polite to you and you will never be inside again. If you stay, I will stay, at this exact distance, for as long as you want. The one person who has ever been closer than this distance was there before the blast.*

This template is **stable, functional, and quietly costly**. It produces an operator who is universally respected, broadly liked, durably partnered, and structurally alone — alone in the specific sense that her interior is housed in one other person and a workload, with no third channel. The file's prognosis stands: she will perform at high level indefinitely, and the day the workload pauses or the Colleen channel closes, the unprocessed thirty years will arrive in a single delivery and require somewhere to go.


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# DOSSIER SECTION — DEFENSES & COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS

## SUBJECT: KNIGHT, MERCEDES "MISTY"

---

## I. Architectural Overview

The defensive architecture of the subject is, in clinical terms, *high-functioning and load-bearing*: it does not merely protect her from anxiety, it *organizes her vocation, her relationships, her gait, her sleep schedule, and the way she enters a room*. The system was largely intact prior to the index trauma — the inferred childhood baseline is securely attached, capability-organized, humor-mediated — but it was *calcified and weaponized* by the blast amputation in young adulthood and then *recalibrated downward in tenderness* by the unprocessed pregnancy loss roughly a decade later. What presents now (modern-era depictions) is an integrated, mature-end-of-the-spectrum defensive stack with a small but consequential floor of more primitive mechanisms that activate only around the two body-domains the conscious system refuses to narrate: the shoulder and the womb.

Ranked from most primitive to most mature, with operational behavior keyed to each:

---

## II. The Primitive Floor (Rare, Domain-Specific, Diagnostic)

### 1. Denial — Bodily Vulnerability Subtype

The most primitive defense in the stack, and the most clinically telling because of how *narrow* its domain is. Subject does not employ denial about the external world, about adversaries, about operational risk, about other people's pathology — she reads all of those with surgical clarity. Denial is reserved for a single subject: **her own body as a vessel rather than a tool.**

Behavioral instantiations:
- Concealment of the pregnancy during the *Daughters of the Dragon* arc — not just from the partner who fathered it but from Colleen Wing, the one person with full access. The concealment is not strategic; it is *not having registered it as real.*
- The complete on-page absence of post-amputation rehabilitation, physical therapy, prosthetic servicing, or medical follow-up across fifty years of publication. A Stark-grade neural interface requires recurrent calibration. Subject is never depicted attending it. The likely truth: she attends grudgingly, briefly, and treats the appointments as administrative.
- The chronic-pain presentation that *must* exist given the kinetic asymmetry of the prosthesis (super-strength right limb attached to baseline-human shoulder girdle and spine) is never named by her, even in private. Inferred behavior: she takes ibuprofen the way some people take coffee, sleeps on the left side to unload the right shoulder, and stretches the trapezius constantly without acknowledging why.

This is denial in the strict Freudian sense — refusal to register an internal fact as a fact. It is also the most psychologically expensive defense in her stack because it leaves the relevant material *unmetabolized* and therefore available to ambush.

### 2. Somatic Dissociation

Adjacent to denial but mechanically distinct. Subject experiences the right side of her body as *not-quite-self*, integrated into identity at the level of *what she does* but partitioned from interoceptive self-monitoring. She can tell you the prosthesis's torque tolerance to the foot-pound and not tell you that her shoulder hurts.

Behavioral signatures:
- Sleeps with the prosthesis on or within reach in a configuration that suggests she has not fully separated *the limb* from *her armed status*. The arm is a weapon; she does not disarm at night.
- Showering, dressing, intimate touch — these are domains where amputees typically renegotiate the body schema. Subject's depicted intimate behavior shows no such renegotiation; the arm is simply present, simply functional, simply not discussed.
- After heavy combat she does not check herself for injury until someone else points to blood. The interoceptive feedback loop is throttled.

### 3. Counterphobic Action (Identification with the Aggressor, Mild)

The script is unmistakable: **she runs toward explosions.** Literally, in the origin event. Figuratively, in case selection — bomb cases, blast-scene investigations, terrorism-adjacent work appear in her docket at a rate well above base for a street-level PI. This is not bravery alone; bravery would tolerate the assignment. Counterphobia *seeks* it.

It is a more primitive defense than the mature-stack items below because it relies on *re-enactment* rather than *processing*. Each successfully survived blast-context tells the nervous system *I am bigger than this*, but the relief is non-cumulative; the next assignment is required to maintain the equilibrium.

---

## III. The Neurotic-Level Mid-Stack (Active Daily)

### 4. Intellectualization

Highly developed in the *adversarial-external* direction; deliberately untrained in the *self-directed* direction. She analyzes other people's defenses with a working clinician's precision — she can tell you in a sentence why Danny dissociates into the Iron Fist persona, why Luke chokes off vulnerability behind volume, why Colleen courts violence after sobriety — and she will refuse to apply the same lens to herself even when explicitly invited.

Operational utility: lets her *handle* damaged people at scale without being destabilized by them. Operational cost: the same machinery, if turned inward, would do the work she most needs done. She is aware of this and treats the awareness itself as sufficient (a meta-defense — *I know I do this, therefore I don't have to stop*).

### 5. Reaction Formation (Narrow, Around Tenderness)

Subject's affectionate impulses toward romantic partners and toward Colleen are reliably present and reliably *over-expressed as ribbing, sarcasm, sharp banter, or physical roughness* (back-slaps, shoves, the playful jab that lands a little hard). The tenderness is real; its packaging is its opposite. This is classic neurotic-tier reaction formation calibrated by cultural and professional context — a Black woman in 1970s NYPD did not survive by being soft in mixed rooms, and the habit became character.

The reaction formation breaks down only with Colleen, in private, in low-stakes moments — kitchen scenes, recovery-after-injury scenes — and even there the softness is brief and quickly re-armored.

### 6. Isolation of Affect

She can recount the bomb, the arm, the miscarriage, Danny's deaths, in flat operational prose. The narrative is intact; the feeling is filed elsewhere. This is not absence of feeling — observable micro-expressions during such recountings (jaw set, brief blink-suppression, a hand-flex of the prosthetic fingers) indicate the affect is firing and being routed to motor rather than to expression.

### 7. Displacement (Onto the Body and Onto the Work)

Unprocessed grief and rage are displaced into two channels: **physical exertion** (she trains harder after losses; the bench-press numbers go up after Danny disappears) and **case intensity** (she takes uglier cases after the miscarriage arc). The displacement is competent enough to be invisible to her and to most observers, including writers across the decades who depict the downstream behavior without naming the upstream cause.

### 8. Rationalization

Used in service of the autonomy drive. Every refusal of help — refusal of medical follow-up, refusal of team-based affiliation past a certain depth, refusal of romantic partner relocation, refusal to take a desk role — is supplied with a clean, internally-consistent professional reason. The reasons are not false; they are *true and sufficient on their own terms* while also performing the defensive function of preventing the underlying material from being addressed.

---

## IV. The Mature Stack (Dominant, Adaptive, Constitutive of Function)

### 9. Sublimation (Master Defense)

The keystone of the entire architecture. Every wound is converted to vocation:

- Lost arm → private investigation agency built on physical capability and street credibility.
- Pregnancy loss → expanded protective behavior toward fragile adults (Danny, Luke, junior operatives in *Heroes for Hire*).
- Institutional betrayal (NYPD's desk-job offer) → institution-building (Knightwing, Daughters of the Dragon partnership, Heroes for Hire handler role).
- Romantic loss → mentorship.
- Chronic untreated rage at the world that wired her this way → competent, ethical violence directed at appropriate targets.

Sublimation is the reason the system *works* despite the primitive floor. It converts what would otherwise be symptom into output, and the output is genuinely good for the city she works in.

### 10. Humor (Wry, Tactical, Caretaking)

The wisecracking register is not personality; it is *tool*. Calibrated uses:
- **Room temperature regulation** — defuses tension in rooms where she is the only Black woman, the only civilian, the only non-powered, or all three.
- **Titration of intimacy with damaged men** — a joke given to Danny or Luke at the right moment is permission for them not to collapse.
- **Self-protection without self-disclosure** — a joke about her arm preempts a sincere question about her arm.
- **Status maintenance against authority** — sarcasm is her preferred upward-management tool with police brass, federal agents, and Stark-tier figures.

The humor reliably escalates as her internal stress rises; it is one of the most readable barometers in her presentation. When the jokes get sharper and faster, the system is approaching its first stress threshold.

### 11. Altruism (Real, Not Pathological)

Distinct from sublimation: this is *genuine other-orientation* not in service of self-regulation. Subject reflexively interposes herself between civilians and harm in contexts where no defensive function is being served. She mentors junior investigators without instrumental benefit. She funds Colleen's various recoveries. The altruism is dispositional, not compensatory, and constitutes evidence for the inferred secure childhood base.

### 12. Anticipation

Highly developed in operational domains, *under*-developed in personal domains. She forecasts adversarial moves, weather, traffic, who will betray whom in a faction, with calm accuracy. She does *not* anticipate her own emotional needs, her own collapse vectors, her own holiday-and-anniversary affective spikes. The anticipation function has been trained outward and starved inward.

### 13. Suppression (vs. Repression — Important Distinction)

Where she is *aware* of an affect and chooses to set it aside for operational reasons, that is suppression and it is healthy. Subject does a great deal of this — she will know she is grieving and decide to grieve next week. The risk is that next week's case arrives and the deferred material accumulates. The suppression is *honest* (she knows what she is doing); the *accumulation* is the pathology.

### 14. Integration (The Prosthesis as Self)

A genuinely mature accomplishment and the brightest single point in her clinical picture: she has integrated the cybernetic limb into self-concept without fetishization, without concealment, and without identity-fragmentation. She does not hide the arm under long sleeves; she does not display it as a trophy; she treats it as *her arm.* This is psychologically expensive work that she has, by all evidence, done — and it is the proof of capacity that the rest of the unprocessed material *could* be metabolized if the conditions for it were ever present.

---

## V. Positive Compensatory Mechanisms (Generative)

Distinct from defenses: these are *constructions* she has built that take the energy of unaddressed material and turn it into durable structure.

- **Institution-building.** Knightwing Restorations, the Daughters of the Dragon partnership, the Heroes for Hire handler infrastructure. Each is a real organization with real beneficiaries, built in the negative space left by the institutions that failed her.
- **The Colleen bond.** A consciously maintained, mutually invested relationship that functions as her external nervous system — co-regulation, accountability, the only relationship in which her defenses are routinely lowered without crisis-precipitation.
